	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 00:27:18 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 00:41:30 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 00:41:30 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 00:55:55 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info

		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 02:04:14 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 02:04:14 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info

		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 03:12:52 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 03:12:52 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 04:20:49 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 04:35:15 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 04:35:16 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas

		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections

		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print

		verbose.output = verbose.output

		SGPt = SGPt

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 05:43:35 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years

		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size

		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 06:38:11 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 06:52:35 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 06:52:35 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 07:07:21 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections

		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print

		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 08:02:37 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 08:02:37 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Thursday February 16 08:17:21 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Thursday February 16 08:17:21 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )
